\begin{titlepage}
\begin{center}
\vspace*{\fill}
{\huge \bfseries \thetitle\par}
\vskip 1.5em
{\Large \theauthor\par}
\vskip 1em
{\large \thedate\par}
\vspace*{\fill}
\end{center}
\end{titlepage}
